""SELECT t.\"UserId\", t.\"BioNote\", t.\"Price\", t.\"UnitOfPrice\", a.\"Id\", t0.\"ID\", t0.\"CreatedOn\", t0.\"IsDepricated\", t0.\"LastModifiedOn\", t0.\"SubjectID\", t0.\"TutorID\", t0.\"ID0\", t0.\"CreatedOn0\", t0.\"EndTime\", t0.\"IsDepricated0\", t0.\"LastModifiedOn0\", t0.\"RateStudent\", t0.\"RateTutor\", t0.\"RatingStudentCount\", t0.\"Startime\", t0.\"Status\", t0.\"StudentId\", t0.\"TutorSubjectID\", t0.\"TutorUserId\", a.\"AccessFailedCount\", a.\"AvatarUrl\", a.\"ConcurrencyStamp\", a.\"Email\", a.\"EmailConfirmed\", a.\"FirstName\", a.\"IsActive\", a.\"LastName\", a.\"LockoutEnabled\", a.\"LockoutEnd\", a.\"NormalizedEmail\", a.\"NormalizedUserName\", a.\"PasswordHash\", a.\"PhoneNumber\", a.\"PhoneNumberConfirmed\", a.\"PublicUrl\", a.\"RefreshToken\", a.\"RefreshTokenExpiryTime\", a.\"SecurityStamp\", a.\"TwoFactorEnabled\", a.\"UserName\"
FROM \"Tutors\" AS t
INNER JOIN \"AspNetUsers\" AS a ON t.\"UserId\" = a.\"Id\"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t1.\"ID\", t1.\"CreatedOn\", t1.\"IsDepricated\", t1.\"LastModifiedOn\", t1.\"SubjectID\", t1.\"TutorID\", s.\"ID\" AS \"ID0\", s.\"CreatedOn\" AS \"CreatedOn0\", s.\"EndTime\", s.\"IsDepricated\" AS \"IsDepricated0\", s.\"LastModifiedOn\" AS \"LastModifiedOn0\", s.\"RateStudent\", s.\"RateTutor\", s.\"RatingStudentCount\", s.\"Startime\", s.\"Status\", s.\"StudentId\", s.\"TutorSubjectID\", s.\"TutorUserId\"

) AS t0 ON t.\"UserId\" = t0.\"TutorID\"
ORDER BY t.\"UserId\", a.\"Id\", t0.\"ID\""

""System.ObjectDisposedException: Cannot access a disposed context instance. A common cause of this error is disposing a context instance that was resolved from dependency injection and then later trying to use the same context instance elsewhere in your application.
